CREATE TABLE STUDENT(
    Sno     CHAR(8),
    Sname   CHAR(10),
    Ssex    CHAR(2),
    Sage    SMALLINT,
    Major   CHAR(20));
CREATE TABLE AWARD( Sno CHAR(8), Details VARCHAR(2000));

SELECT A.Sno, Sname, Ssex, Sage, Major, Details /*Êü•ËØ¢Â≠¶Âè∑‰∏∫20100001 Â≠¶ÁîüÁöÑ‰ø°ÊÅØ*/
FROM STUDENT A LEFT JOIN AWARD B ON A.Sno=B.Sno
WHERE A.Sno = '20100001'
